			add_to_variable = { MOT_BasicPower_of_Trader = -5 }

			set_country_flag = MOT_Reform_Poli

					flag = MOT_Reform_Poli

			has_global_flag = MOT_REUNITED

				add = 1000

				add = -1000

					rule = MOT_ChoosetheWay

				}

		}

					}

				}
				ELSE_IF = {
					create_faction = Global_Facist_Camp
					set_country_flag = facist_camp_founder

					unlock_decision_category_tooltip = Faction_Helper
					set_country_flag = Faction_Help_On
				}
			}

	#根据工业总值获得建筑槽奖励 x38 y9
	#蓝 工业革新
	focus = {
		id = MOT_EcoB_End
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_production2
		cost = 10
		x = 38
		y = 9
		completion_reward = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MOT_ExtraBonus_From_Industry
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_war_support = 0.1
			every_military_industrial_organization = {
				add_mio_size = 1
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					num_of_factories > 200
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MOT_ExtraBonus_From_200
				every_military_industrial_organization = {
					add_mio_size = 1
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					category = industry
					uses = 1
					ahead_reduction = 2
					bonus = 1
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					num_of_factories > 300
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MOT_ExtraBonus_From_300
				every_military_industrial_organization = {
					add_mio_size = 1
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					category = cat_mechanized_equipment
					uses = 1
					ahead_reduction = 2
					bonus = 1
				}
				add_tech_bonus = {
					category = night_vision
					uses = 1
					ahead_reduction = 2
					bonus = 1
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					num_of_factories > 400
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MOT_ExtraBonus_From_400
				every_military_industrial_organization = {
					add_mio_size = 1
				}
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_war_support = 0.1
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_state_category = wasteland } }
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					num_of_factories > 500
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MOT_ExtraBonus_From_500
				every_military_industrial_organization = {
					add_mio_size = 1
				}
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_war_support = 0.1
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_state_category = wasteland } }
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { 
						free_building_slots = {
						building = infrastructure
							level > 0
						}
					}
					add_building_construction = {
						type = infrastructure
						level = 1
					}
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					num_of_factories > 600
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MOT_ExtraBonus_From_600
				every_military_industrial_organization = {
					add_mio_size = 1
				}
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_war_support = 0.1
				add_research_slots = 1
				add_ideas = DOT_Government_Industry5
			}
		}
		prerequisite = {
			focus = MOT_EcoB_Cons_Arms_4
			focus = MOT_EcoB_Cons_All_4
			focus = MOT_EcoB_Cons_Civil_4
		}
		available = {
		}
		cancel_if_invalid = yes
		continue_if_invalid = no
		available_if_capitulated = no
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
		}
